🤖 CLAUDE:
Проблема: `<webview src={url}>` загружает URL мгновенно при mount, даже если webview ещё не ready. При переключении на terminal view — `ERR_ABORTED`. Решение: lazy load через `dom-ready` + error page.

🤖 CLAUDE:

**Actions:**
📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/renderer/components/Workspace/BrowserTab.tsx)
```
import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback, memo } from 'react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '../../store/useWorkspaceStore';
import { RotateCcw, ArrowLeft, ArrowRight, Globe, TerminalSquare, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import Terminal from './Terminal';

interface BrowserTabProps {
  tabId: string;
  url: string;
  active: boolean;
  isActiveProject: boolean;
  terminalId?: string;
  terminalName?: string;
  activeView?: 'browser' | 'terminal';
  cwd: string;
}

function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
  const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
  const domReadyRef = useRef(false);
  const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(url || 'http://localhost:3000');
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const updateTabUrl = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.updateTabUrl);
  const setBrowserActiveView = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.setBrowserActiveView);

  // Sync address bar when url prop changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (url) {
      setAddressValue(url);
    }
  }, [url]);

  // Webview event listeners + lazy load
  useEffect(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (!webview) return;

    const handleDomReady = () => {
      domReadyRef.current = true;
      // Load the actual URL after webview is ready
      const targetUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
      webview.loadURL(targetUrl).catch(() => {
        // loadURL rejection is handled by did-fail-load
      });
    };

    const handleStartLoading = () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setLoadError(null);
    };
    const handleStopLoading = () => setIsLoading(false);
    const handleNavigate = (e: any) => {
      setAddressValue(e.url);
      updateTabUrl(tabId, e.url);
    };
    const handleFailLoad = (e: any) => {
      // Ignore aborted loads (user navigated away, view switched) and cancelled
      // errorCode -3 = ERR_ABORTED, -27 = ERR_HOST_RESOLVER_QUEUE_TOO_LARGE
      if (e.errorCode === -3 || e.errorCode === 0) return;
      setLoadError(`${e.errorDescription || 'Connection failed'} (${e.validatedURL})`);
      setIsLoading(false);
    };

    webview.addEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    webview.addEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    webview.addEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    webview.addEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);

    return () => {
      webview.removeEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    };
  }, [tabId, url, updateTabUrl]);

  const navigateTo = useCallback((targetUrl: string) => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (!webview || !domReadyRef.current) return;
    setLoadError(null);
    webview.loadURL(targetUrl).catch(() => {});
  }, []);

  const handleAddressSubmit = useCallback((e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    let navigateUrl = addressValue.trim();
    if (!navigateUrl) return;

    if (!navigateUrl.match(/^https?:\/\//)) {
      navigateUrl = 'http://' + navigateUrl;
    }

    setAddressValue(navigateUrl);
    updateTabUrl(tabId, navigateUrl);
    navigateTo(navigateUrl);
  }, [addressValue, tabId, updateTabUrl, navigateTo]);

  const handleRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && domReadyRef.current) {
      setLoadError(null);
      webview.reload();
    }
  }, []);

  const handleGoBack = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && domReadyRef.current && webview.canGoBack()) {
      webview.goBack();
    }
  }, []);

  const handleGoForward = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && domReadyRef.current && webview.canGoForward()) {
      webview.goForward();
    }
  }, []);

  const isVisible = active && isActiveProject;
  const isBrowserView = activeView === 'browser';
  const isTerminalView = activeView === 'terminal';

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        position: 'absolute',
        inset: 0,
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        visibility: isVisible ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
        pointerEvents: isVisible ? 'auto' : 'none',
        zIndex: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
      }}
    >
      {/* Toolbar - 30px */}
      <div
        style={{
          height: '30px',
          minHeight: '30px',
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          gap: '4px',
          padding: '0 8px',
          backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
          borderBottom: '1px solid #333',
        }}
      >
        {/* Nav buttons */}
        <button
          onClick={handleGoBack}
          style={{
            background: 'none',
            border: 'none',
            color: '#888',
            cursor: 'pointer',
            padding: '2px',
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
          }}
          title="Back"
        >
          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={handleGoForward}
          style={{
            background: 'none',
            border: 'none',
            color: '#888',
            cursor: 'pointer',
            padding: '2px',
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
          }}
          title="Forward"
        >
          <ArrowRight size={14} />
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={handleRefresh}
          style={{
            background: 'none',
            border: 'none',
            color: '#888',
            cursor: 'pointer',
            padding: '2px',
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
          }}
          title="Refresh"
        >
          <RotateCcw size={14} className={isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />
        </button>

        {/* URL input */}
        <form onSubmit={handleAddressSubmit} style={{ flex: 1 }}>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={addressValue}
            onChange={(e) => setAddressValue(e.target.value)}
            onFocus={(e) => e.target.select()}
            style={{
              width: '100%',
              height: '22px',
              backgroundColor: '#252525',
              border: `1px solid ${loadError ? '#ef4444' : '#444'}`,
              borderRadius: '4px',
              color: '#ccc',
              fontSize: '12px',
              padding: '0 8px',
              outline: 'none',
            }}
            placeholder="http://localhost:3000"
          />
        </form>

        {/* Sub-tab switcher */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '2px', marginLeft: '4px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'browser')}
            style={{
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              gap: '4px',
              padding: '2px 8px',
              height: '22px',
              borderRadius: '4px',
              border: 'none',
              fontSize: '11px',
              cursor: 'pointer',
              backgroundColor: isBrowserView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
              color: isBrowserView ? '#fff' : '#888',
              transition: 'all 0.15s',
            }}
            title="Browser view"
          >
            <Globe size={12} />
            <span>Browser</span>
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'terminal')}
            style={{
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              gap: '4px',
              padding: '2px 8px',
              height: '22px',
              borderRadius: '4px',
              border: 'none',
              fontSize: '11px',
              cursor: 'pointer',
              backgroundColor: isTerminalView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
              color: isTerminalView ? '#fff' : '#888',
              transition: 'all 0.15s',
            }}
            title="Terminal view"
          >
            <TerminalSquare size={12} />
            <span>Term</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content area */}
      <div style={{ flex: 1, position: 'relative' }}>
        {/* Webview */}
        <div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            inset: 0,
            visibility: isBrowserView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
            pointerEvents: isBrowserView ? 'auto' : 'none',
            zIndex: isBrowserView ? 1 : 0,
          }}
        >
          {/* No src — loaded programmatically after dom-ready to avoid ERR_ABORTED */}
          <webview
            ref={webviewRef}
            src="about:blank"
            style={{
              width: '100%',
              height: '100%',
              border: 'none',
            }}
            {...{ allowpopups: '' } as any}
          />

          {/* Error overlay */}
          {loadError && isBrowserView && (
            <div
              style={{
                position: 'absolute',
                inset: 0,
                display: 'flex',
                flexDirection: 'column',
                alignItems: 'center',
                justifyContent: 'center',
                backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
                gap: '12px',
              }}
            >
              <AlertTriangle size={32} color="#ef4444" />
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '13px', textAlign: 'center', maxWidth: '400px', padding: '0 20px' }}>
                {loadError}
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={handleRefresh}
                style={{
                  padding: '6px 16px',
                  backgroundColor: '#333',
                  border: '1px solid #555',
                  borderRadius: '6px',
                  color: '#ccc',
                  fontSize: '12px',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                }}
              >
                Retry
              </button>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Embedded Terminal */}
        {terminalId && (
          <div
            style={{
              position: 'absolute',
              inset: 0,
              visibility: isTerminalView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
              pointerEvents: isTerminalView ? 'auto' : 'none',
              zIndex: isTerminalView ? 1 : 0,
            }}
          >
            <Terminal
              tabId={terminalId}
              cwd={cwd}
              active={active && isTerminalView}
              isActiveProject={isActiveProject}
            />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default memo(BrowserTab);

```

```
/**
 * Test: Browser Tab — Create, Switch Views, Error Handling
 *
 * Проверяет:
 * 1. Кнопка Globe создаёт browser tab (tabType === 'browser')
 * 2. Tab дефолтно открывается в browser view (activeView === 'browser')
 * 3. Webview рендерится (dom-ready)
 * 4. Переключение Browser ↔ Terminal работает без ошибок
 * 5. Terminal view содержит рабочий xterm.js
 * 6. Нет uncaught errors (ERR_ABORTED, reload is not a function)
 *
 * Запуск: node auto/sandbox/test-browser-tab.js
 */

const { launch, waitForTerminal } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

const c = {
  reset: '\x1b[0m',
  green: '\x1b[32m',
  red: '\x1b[31m',
  cyan: '\x1b[36m',
  yellow: '\x1b[33m',
  dim: '\x1b[2m'
}

const log = {
  step: (msg) => console.log(`${c.cyan}[STEP]${c.reset} ${msg}`),
  pass: (msg) => console.log(`${c.green}[PASS]${c.reset} ${msg}`),
  fail: (msg) => console.log(`${c.red}[FAIL]${c.reset} ${msg}`),
  warn: (msg) => console.log(`${c.yellow}[WARN]${c.reset} ${msg}`),
  info: (msg) => console.log(`${c.dim}[INFO]${c.reset} ${msg}`)
}

// Collect uncaught errors from renderer
const uncaughtErrors = []

async function main() {
  log.step('Запуск Noted Terminal...')

  const { app, page, consoleLogs, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false,
    logMainProcess: false,
    waitForReady: 4000
  })

  log.pass('Приложение запущено')

  // Track page errors (uncaught exceptions)
  page.on('pageerror', (err) => {
    uncaughtErrors.push(err.message)
  })

  try {
    // ===== SETUP =====
    log.step('Ожидание терминала...')
    await waitForTerminal(page, 15000)
    log.pass('Терминал активен')

    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(500)

    // ===== TEST 1: Создание browser tab =====
    log.step('Клик по кнопке Globe (Open browser tab)...')

    // Find the Globe button in ProjectToolbar
    const globeButton = page.locator('button[title="Open browser tab"]')
    const globeVisible = await globeButton.isVisible().catch(() => false)

    if (!globeVisible) {
      log.fail('Кнопка Globe не найдена в toolbar')
      return
    }

    await globeButton.click()
    await page.waitForTimeout(2000) // PTY spawn + webview init

    log.pass('Кнопка Globe нажата')

    // ===== TEST 2: Проверка tab state =====
    log.step('Проверка tab state в store...')

    const tabState = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const store = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      if (!store) return null
      const proj = store.openProjects?.get?.(store.activeProjectId)
      if (!proj) return null
      const tab = proj.tabs?.get?.(proj.activeTabId)
      return tab ? {
        id: tab.id,
        name: tab.name,
        tabType: tab.tabType,
        url: tab.url,
        activeView: tab.activeView,
      } : null
    })

    log.info(`Tab state: ${JSON.stringify(tabState)}`)

    if (tabState?.tabType === 'browser') {
      log.pass('tabType === "browser"')
    } else {
      log.fail(`tabType: ${tabState?.tabType || 'undefined'} (expected "browser")`)
    }

    // ===== TEST 3: Webview рендерится =====
    log.step('Проверка наличия webview в DOM...')

    const webviewExists = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const wv = document.querySelector('webview')
      return !!wv
    })

    if (webviewExists) {
      log.pass('Webview присутствует в DOM')
    } else {
      log.fail('Webview не найден в DOM')
    }

    // ===== TEST 4: Browser view активен по умолчанию =====
    log.step('Проверка дефолтного view...')

    // Check that Browser button is highlighted (active)
    const browserBtnActive = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const btns = document.querySelectorAll('button[title="Browser view"]')
      for (const btn of btns) {
        const style = btn.getAttribute('style') || ''
        if (style.includes('rgba(255')) return true
      }
      return false
    })

    if (browserBtnActive) {
      log.pass('Browser view активен по умолчанию')
    } else {
      log.warn('Browser view может быть не активен (проверьте визуально)')
    }

    // ===== TEST 5: Переключение на Terminal view =====
    log.step('Переключение на Terminal view...')

    const termButton = page.locator('button[title="Terminal view"]')
    await termButton.click()
    await page.waitForTimeout(1500)

    // Check that terminal rendered
    const hasTerminal = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const screens = document.querySelectorAll('.xterm-screen')
      // At least one visible xterm-screen
      for (const s of screens) {
        const rect = s.getBoundingClientRect()
        if (rect.width > 0 && rect.height > 0) return true
      }
      return false
    })

    if (hasTerminal) {
      log.pass('Terminal view содержит xterm.js')
    } else {
      log.warn('Terminal view: xterm-screen не виден (может быть ещё не инициализирован)')
    }

    // ===== TEST 6: Переключение обратно на Browser view =====
    log.step('Переключение обратно на Browser view...')

    const browserButton = page.locator('button[title="Browser view"]')
    await browserButton.click()
    await page.waitForTimeout(1000)

    // Check store activeView
    const viewAfterSwitch = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const store = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const proj = store?.openProjects?.get?.(store?.activeProjectId)
      const tab = proj?.tabs?.get?.(proj?.activeTabId)
      return tab?.activeView
    })

    if (viewAfterSwitch === 'browser') {
      log.pass('activeView === "browser" после переключения')
    } else {
      log.fail(`activeView: ${viewAfterSwitch} (expected "browser")`)
    }

    // ===== TEST 7: Ввод URL и навигация =====
    log.step('Ввод URL в адресную строку...')

    const urlInput = page.locator('input[placeholder="http://localhost:3000"]')
    const inputVisible = await urlInput.isVisible().catch(() => false)

    if (inputVisible) {
      await urlInput.click()
      await urlInput.fill('http://localhost:5173')
      await page.keyboard.press('Enter')
      await page.waitForTimeout(2000)

      // Check address bar updated
      const currentUrl = await urlInput.inputValue()
      if (currentUrl.includes('localhost:5173') || currentUrl.includes('localhost')) {
        log.pass(`URL updated: ${currentUrl}`)
      } else {
        log.warn(`URL may not have updated: ${currentUrl}`)
      }
    } else {
      log.warn('URL input не найден')
    }

    // ===== TEST 8: Нет uncaught errors =====
    log.step('Проверка uncaught errors...')

    // Filter out benign errors
    const criticalErrors = uncaughtErrors.filter(e =>
      !e.includes('ERR_ABORTED') &&       // Expected when view switches during load
      !e.includes('ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED') // Expected if localhost not running
    )

    if (criticalErrors.length === 0) {
      log.pass(`Нет критических uncaught errors (benign: ${uncaughtErrors.length})`)
    } else {
      log.fail(`Критические errors (${criticalErrors.length}):`)
      criticalErrors.forEach(e => log.info(`  ${e}`))
    }

    // Check for "reload is not a function" specifically
    const reloadError = uncaughtErrors.find(e => e.includes('reload is not a function'))
    if (!reloadError) {
      log.pass('Нет ошибки "reload is not a function" (webviewTag enabled)')
    } else {
      log.fail('Ошибка "reload is not a function" — webviewTag не включён?')
    }

    // ===== ИТОГО =====
    console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════')

    const results = {
      browserTabCreated: tabState?.tabType === 'browser',
      webviewInDom: webviewExists,
      noReloadError: !reloadError,
      noCriticalErrors: criticalErrors.length === 0,
      viewSwitchWorks: viewAfterSwitch === 'browser',
    }

    const allPassed = Object.values(results).every(Boolean)

    if (allPassed) {
      log.pass('ТЕСТ ПРОЙДЕН: Browser Tab работает корректно')
    } else {
      log.fail('ТЕСТ НЕ ПРОЙДЕН:')
      for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(results)) {
        if (!val) log.fail(`  ${key}: FAILED`)
      }
    }

    console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════')

    // Dump errors if any
    if (uncaughtErrors.length > 0) {
      console.log('\n--- All Uncaught Errors ---')
      uncaughtErrors.forEach(e => log.info(e))
      console.log('--- End ---\n')
    }

  } finally {
    log.step('Закрытие приложения...')
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => {
  console.error(`${c.red}[ERROR]${c.reset}`, err.message)
  console.error(err.stack)
  process.exit(1)
})

📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/src/renderer/components/Workspace/BrowserTab.tsx)
```
import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback, memo } from 'react';
import { useWorkspaceStore } from '../../store/useWorkspaceStore';
import { RotateCcw, ArrowLeft, ArrowRight, Globe, TerminalSquare, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import Terminal from './Terminal';

interface BrowserTabProps {
  tabId: string;
  url: string;
  active: boolean;
  isActiveProject: boolean;
  terminalId?: string;
  terminalName?: string;
  activeView?: 'browser' | 'terminal';
  cwd: string;
}

function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
  const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
  const initialUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
  const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(initialUrl);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
  const updateTabUrl = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.updateTabUrl);
  const setBrowserActiveView = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.setBrowserActiveView);

  // Sync address bar when url prop changes (ignore about:blank)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (url && url !== 'about:blank') {
      setAddressValue(url);
    }
  }, [url]);

  // Webview event listeners
  useEffect(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (!webview) return;

    const handleDomReady = () => setIsReady(true);
    const handleStartLoading = () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setLoadError(null);
    };
    const handleStopLoading = () => setIsLoading(false);
    const handleNavigate = (e: any) => {
      // Skip about:blank — don't overwrite real URL in store
      if (e.url === 'about:blank') return;
      setAddressValue(e.url);
      updateTabUrl(tabId, e.url);
    };
    const handleFailLoad = (e: any) => {
      // -3 = ERR_ABORTED (user navigated away / view switched) — benign
      // 0 = no error
      if (e.errorCode === -3 || e.errorCode === 0) return;
      setLoadError(`${e.errorDescription || 'Connection failed'} (${e.validatedURL})`);
      setIsLoading(false);
    };

    webview.addEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    webview.addEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    webview.addEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    webview.addEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);

    return () => {
      webview.removeEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
      webview.removeEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    };
  }, [tabId, updateTabUrl]);

  const handleAddressSubmit = useCallback((e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    let navigateUrl = addressValue.trim();
    if (!navigateUrl) return;

    if (!navigateUrl.match(/^https?:\/\//)) {
      navigateUrl = 'http://' + navigateUrl;
    }

    setAddressValue(navigateUrl);
    updateTabUrl(tabId, navigateUrl);
    setLoadError(null);

    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && isReady) {
      webview.src = navigateUrl;
    }
  }, [addressValue, tabId, updateTabUrl, isReady]);

  const handleRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && isReady) {
      setLoadError(null);
      webview.reload();
    }
  }, [isReady]);

  const handleGoBack = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoBack()) {
      webview.goBack();
    }
  }, [isReady]);

  const handleGoForward = useCallback(() => {
    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoForward()) {
      webview.goForward();
    }
  }, [isReady]);

  const isVisible = active && isActiveProject;
  const isBrowserView = activeView === 'browser';
  const isTerminalView = activeView === 'terminal';

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        position: 'absolute',
        inset: 0,
        display: 'flex',
        flexDirection: 'column',
        visibility: isVisible ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
        pointerEvents: isVisible ? 'auto' : 'none',
        zIndex: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
      }}
    >
      {/* Toolbar - 30px */}
      <div
        style={{
          height: '30px',
          minHeight: '30px',
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          gap: '4px',
          padding: '0 8px',
          backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
          borderBottom: '1px solid #333',
        }}
      >
        <button
          onClick={handleGoBack}
          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
          title="Back"
        >
          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={handleGoForward}
          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
          title="Forward"
        >
          <ArrowRight size={14} />
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={handleRefresh}
          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
          title="Refresh"
        >
          <RotateCcw size={14} className={isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />
        </button>

        <form onSubmit={handleAddressSubmit} style={{ flex: 1 }}>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={addressValue}
            onChange={(e) => setAddressValue(e.target.value)}
            onFocus={(e) => e.target.select()}
            style={{
              width: '100%',
              height: '22px',
              backgroundColor: '#252525',
              border: `1px solid ${loadError ? '#ef4444' : '#444'}`,
              borderRadius: '4px',
              color: '#ccc',
              fontSize: '12px',
              padding: '0 8px',
              outline: 'none',
            }}
            placeholder="http://localhost:3000"
          />
        </form>

        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '2px', marginLeft: '4px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'browser')}
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
              backgroundColor: isBrowserView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
              color: isBrowserView ? '#fff' : '#888', transition: 'all 0.15s',
            }}
            title="Browser view"
          >
            <Globe size={12} />
            <span>Browser</span>
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'terminal')}
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
              backgroundColor: isTerminalView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
              color: isTerminalView ? '#fff' : '#888', transition: 'all 0.15s',
            }}
            title="Terminal view"
          >
            <TerminalSquare size={12} />
            <span>Term</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Content area */}
      <div style={{ flex: 1, position: 'relative' }}>
        {/* Webview — src set directly, errors handled via did-fail-load */}
        <div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            inset: 0,
            visibility: isBrowserView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
            pointerEvents: isBrowserView ? 'auto' : 'none',
            zIndex: isBrowserView ? 1 : 0,
          }}
        >
          <webview
            ref={webviewRef}
            src={initialUrl}
            style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', border: 'none' }}
            {...{ allowpopups: '' } as any}
          />

          {/* Error overlay */}
          {loadError && isBrowserView && (
            <div
              style={{
                position: 'absolute', inset: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column',
                alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a', gap: '12px',
              }}
            >
              <AlertTriangle size={32} color="#ef4444" />
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '13px', textAlign: 'center', maxWidth: '400px', padding: '0 20px' }}>
                {loadError}
              </div>
              <button
                onClick={handleRefresh}
                style={{
                  padding: '6px 16px', backgroundColor: '#333', border: '1px solid #555',
                  borderRadius: '6px', color: '#ccc', fontSize: '12px', cursor: 'pointer',
                }}
              >
                Retry
              </button>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Embedded Terminal */}
        {terminalId && (
          <div
            style={{
              position: 'absolute',
              inset: 0,
              visibility: isTerminalView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
              pointerEvents: isTerminalView ? 'auto' : 'none',
              zIndex: isTerminalView ? 1 : 0,
            }}
          >
            <Terminal
              tabId={terminalId}
              cwd={cwd}
              active={active && isTerminalView}
              isActiveProject={isActiveProject}
            />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export default memo(BrowserTab);

```

🤖 CLAUDE:
Понял, закрыл потому что зависло. Это из-за моего `loadURL` подхода — он крэшил renderer. Я уже откатил на `src={initialUrl}` напрямую (без `about:blank` + `loadURL`).

Ключевое отличие от предыдущей версии:
1. `src={initialUrl}` — прямая загрузка, как было
2. `did-fail-load` — ловит ошибки, показывает error overlay вместо крэша
3. `handleNavigate` — пропускает `about:blank` (не перезаписывает URL в store)
4. `isReady` guard — `reload()`, `goBack()` etc. вызываются только после `dom-ready`

Давай перезапущу тест на обновлённой версии:

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - User reported `Uncaught TypeError: webview.reload is not a function` error on the browser tab button (Globe icon)
   - Neither terminal nor browser worked correctly in browser tabs
   - User then reported `ERR_ABORTED (-3)` error when switching between browser and terminal views
   - User explicitly requested to read `auto/context.md` and write tests following that methodology
   - User confirmed `http://localhost:5173/` works but browser tab doesn't open it

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Electron `<webview>` tag requires explicit `webviewTag: true` in `webPreferences` - without it the element renders as dead HTML with no API
   - `visibility: 'visible'` on children overrides parent `visibility: 'hidden'` — must use `'inherit'` (documented in `docs/knowledge/ui-ux-stability.md` section 11.1)
   - Electron webview `did-fail-load` event with `errorCode === -3` (ERR_ABORTED) is benign — happens when navigation is cancelled during view switch
   - Webview `loadURL()` after `src="about:blank"` crashes the Electron renderer — do NOT use lazy loading pattern with about:blank
   - Browser tabs share PTY identity with the tab itself (`tab.id` IS the terminal ID since `createTab` creates PTY with `tabId`)
   - Playwright strict mode requires unique selectors — hidden BrowserTab instances from other tabs create duplicate buttons in DOM
   - Test infrastructure at `auto/` uses event-driven patterns with Zustand store access via `page.evaluate()` for reliable assertions
   - Persisted state (SQLite) means previous test runs affect next test startup (browser tab becomes active tab)

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`src/main/main.js` (line ~314)**
     - Critical fix: webviewTag was missing from BrowserWindow webPreferences
     - Without this, `<webview>` renders as empty HTML element, no `.reload()`, `.canGoBack()` etc.
     ```javascript
     webPreferences: {
       nodeIntegration: true,
       contextIsolation: false,
       webviewTag: true,  // ADDED — enables <webview> tag API
     },
     ```

   - **`src/renderer/components/Workspace/TerminalArea.tsx` (lines 217-229)**
     - Two fixes in the BrowserTab rendering section
     - `terminalId` was always undefined because `createBrowserTab` never sets `tab.terminalId`; the PTY is created with `tab.id`
     - Default `activeView` was 'terminal', meaning browser tab opened showing empty terminal view
     ```jsx
     if (tab.tabType === 'browser') {
       result.push(
         <BrowserTab
           key={tab.id}
           tabId={tab.id}
           url={tab.url || 'http://localhost:3000'}
           active={isActive}
           isActiveProject={isActiveProject}
           terminalId={tab.terminalId || tab.id}  // CHANGED: was tab.terminalId (undefined)
           terminalName={tab.terminalName}
           activeView={tab.activeView || 'browser'}  // CHANGED: was 'terminal'
           cwd={tab.cwd}
         />
       );
     }
     ```

   - **`src/renderer/components/Workspace/BrowserTab.tsx`** — Full rewrite
     - Added `did-fail-load` handler that ignores ERR_ABORTED (-3) and shows error overlay for real failures
     - Added `dom-ready` tracking via `isReady` state — guards all webview API calls
     - `handleNavigate` skips `about:blank` URL to prevent overwriting real URL in store
     - Changed all `visibility: 'visible'` to `'inherit'` (3 places: outer container, webview wrapper, terminal wrapper)
     - Default `activeView` prop changed from `'terminal'` to `'browser'`
     - Uses direct `src={initialUrl}` (NOT lazy `about:blank` + `loadURL` which crashes renderer)
     - Error overlay with AlertTriangle icon + Retry button
     ```tsx
     function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
       const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
       const initialUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
       const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(initialUrl);
       const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
       const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
       const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
       // ... handlers with isReady guards, did-fail-load, handleNavigate skipping about:blank
       // <webview ref={webviewRef} src={initialUrl} ... />  — direct src, not lazy
     }
     ```

   - **`auto/sandbox/test-browser-tab.js`** — New test file
     - Tests: browser tab creation, tabType in store, webview in DOM, default browser view, terminal view switch, browser view switch back, no uncaught errors, no "reload is not a function"
     - Uses store-based view switching (`page.evaluate(() => store.setBrowserActiveView(...))`) instead of DOM button clicks to avoid strict mode violations from hidden duplicate buttons
     - Handles persisted browser tab from previous test runs by checking `currentTabType` and creating new terminal tab if needed
     - Follows patterns from `auto/stable/test-sniper-handshake.js`: colors, log helpers, try/finally, waitForTerminal, electron.focusWindow

   - **`src/renderer/store/useWorkspaceStore.ts` (lines 1289-1319)** — Read only
     - `createBrowserTab` creates tab with `tabType: 'browser'`, `url: 'http://localhost:3000'` but no `terminalId`
     - `setBrowserActiveView` mutates `tab.activeView` and triggers re-render
     - `updateTabUrl` mutates `tab.url` in store

   - **Knowledge/docs files read**: All 12 knowledge files, architecture.md, main-feature.md, all auto/ infrastructure files (context.md, playwright/basics.md, playwright/electron.md, core/launcher.js, core/electron.js, libraries/xterm.md, libraries/zustand-store.md, stable/test-sniper-handshake.js)

    17→function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
    18→  const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
    19→  const initialUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
    20→  const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(initialUrl);
    21→  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    22→  const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    23→  const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
    24→  const updateTabUrl = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.updateTabUrl);
    25→  const setBrowserActiveView = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.setBrowserActiveView);
    26→
    27→  // Sync address bar when url prop changes (ignore about:blank)
    28→  useEffect(() => {
    29→    if (url && url !== 'about:blank') {
    30→      setAddressValue(url);
    31→    }
    32→  }, [url]);
    33→
    34→  // Webview event listeners
    35→  useEffect(() => {
    36→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    37→    if (!webview) return;
    38→
    39→    const handleDomReady = () => setIsReady(true);
    40→    const handleStartLoading = () => {
    41→      setIsLoading(true);
    42→      setLoadError(null);
    43→    };
    44→    const handleStopLoading = () => setIsLoading(false);
    45→    const handleNavigate = (e: any) => {
    46→      // Skip about:blank — don't overwrite real URL in store
    47→      if (e.url === 'about:blank') return;
    48→      setAddressValue(e.url);
    49→      updateTabUrl(tabId, e.url);
    50→    };
    51→    const handleFailLoad = (e: any) => {
    52→      // -3 = ERR_ABORTED (user navigated away / view switched) — benign
    53→      // 0 = no error
    54→      if (e.errorCode === -3 || e.errorCode === 0) return;
    55→      setLoadError(`${e.errorDescription || 'Connection failed'} (${e.validatedURL})`);
    56→      setIsLoading(false);
    57→    };
    58→
    59→    webview.addEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    60→    webview.addEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    61→    webview.addEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    62→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    63→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    64→    webview.addEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    65→
    66→    return () => {
    67→      webview.removeEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    68→      webview.removeEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    69→      webview.removeEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    70→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    71→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    72→      webview.removeEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    73→    };
    74→  }, [tabId, updateTabUrl]);
    75→
    76→  const handleAddressSubmit = useCallback((e: React.FormEvent) => {
    77→    e.preventDefault();
    78→    let navigateUrl = addressValue.trim();
    79→    if (!navigateUrl) return;
    80→
    81→    if (!navigateUrl.match(/^https?:\/\//)) {
    82→      navigateUrl = 'http://' + navigateUrl;
    83→    }
    84→
    85→    setAddressValue(navigateUrl);
    86→    updateTabUrl(tabId, navigateUrl);
    87→    setLoadError(null);
    88→
    89→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    90→    if (webview && isReady) {
    91→      webview.src = navigateUrl;
    92→    }
    93→  }, [addressValue, tabId, updateTabUrl, isReady]);
    94→
    95→  const handleRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    96→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    97→    if (webview && isReady) {
    98→      setLoadError(null);
    99→      webview.reload();
   100→    }
   101→  }, [isReady]);
   102→
   103→  const handleGoBack = useCallback(() => {
   104→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   105→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoBack()) {
   106→      webview.goBack();
   107→    }
   108→  }, [isReady]);
   109→
   110→  const handleGoForward = useCallback(() => {
   111→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   112→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoForward()) {
   113→      webview.goForward();
   114→    }
   115→  }, [isReady]);
   116→
   117→  const isVisible = active && isActiveProject;
   118→  const isBrowserView = activeView === 'browser';
   119→  const isTerminalView = activeView === 'terminal';
   120→
   121→  return (
   122→    <div
   123→      style={{
   124→        position: 'absolute',
   125→        inset: 0,
   126→        display: 'flex',

   136→          height: '30px',

   139→          alignItems: 'center',
   140→          gap: '4px',
   141→          padding: '0 8px',
   142→          backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
   143→          borderBottom: '1px solid #333',
   144→        }}
   145→      >
   146→        <button
   147→          onClick={handleGoBack}
   148→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   149→          title="Back"
   150→        >
   151→          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
   152→        </button>
   153→        <button
   154→          onClick={handleGoForward}

🤖 CLAUDE:
<thinking>
Now I see the full picture. The issue is clear:

1. **Webview steals focus**: The `<webview>` in Electron is a separate `WebContents`. Even with `visibility: hidden` and `pointerEvents: none`, it can still hold keyboard focus. When the user switches to terminal view, the terminal calls `term.focus()`, but the webview's `WebContents` may still have system-level focus, intercepting keyboard events before they reach the xterm.js canvas.

2. **ERR_ABORTED**: When switching views, if the webview is s...[truncated]
</thinking>

🤖 CLAUDE:
Я проверил файлы: `BrowserTab.tsx`, `Terminal.tsx`, `TerminalArea.tsx`

**Constraints:**
- `Terminal.tsx:311` — `effectiveActive` = `active && projectCurrentView === 'terminal' && workspaceView === 'workspace'` — правильно вычисляется, `term.focus()` вызывается на line 1308
- Electron `<webview>` — это отдельный `WebContents`. `visibility: hidden` + `pointerEvents: none` не снимают keyboard focus с WebContents. Webview перехватывает клавиатуру до xterm.js
- ERR_ABORTED (-3) — из Electron `GUEST_VIEW_MANAGER_CALL`, не из нашего `did-fail-load`. Console noise, не подавляется

Проблема: при переключении на Terminal, webview **не теряет фокус** — нужен явный `webview.blur()`.

  1300→      if (tab) {
  1301→        tab.url = url;
  1302→        saveTabs(workspace.projectId, workspace.tabs);
  1303→        return;
  1304→      }
  1305→    }
  1306→  },

  1316→        return;
  1317→      }
  1318→    }
  1319→  },

<thinking>
Now I see the full picture:

1. `createBrowserTab` calls `createTab(projectId, 'Browser', cwd, { tabType: 'browser', url: 'http://localhost:3000' })`
2. `createTab` creates a PTY via `ipcRenderer.invoke('terminal:create', { tabId, cwd, rows: 24, cols: 80 })`
3. The PTY is created with `tabId` as its identifier
4. The shell starts running in the PTY immediately

- Gets `tabId={terminalId}` where `terminalId = tab.terminalId || tab.id = tab.id`

   410→        if (pendingAction) {
   411→          console.log('[Terminal:handleData] First PTY output, executing pendingAction');

   416→      // If xterm not yet created, buffer data for later replay
   417→      if (!xtermInstance.current) {
   418→        pendingBuffer.current += payload.data;
   419→        // Limit buffer size to prevent memory issues
   420→        if (pendingBuffer.current.length > 100000) {
   421→          pendingBuffer.current = pendingBuffer.current.slice(-50000);
   422→        }
   423→        return;
   424→      }
   425→
   426→      // Accumulate data in buffer
   427→      writeBufferRef.current += payload.data;
   428→
   429→      // Schedule flush if not already pending
   430→      if (!pendingWriteRef.current) {
   431→        pendingWriteRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
   432→          if (xtermInstance.current && writeBufferRef.current) {
   433→            xtermInstance.current.write(writeBufferRef.current);
   434→            writeBufferRef.current = '';
   435→          }
   436→          pendingWriteRef.current = null;
   437→        }, FLUSH_DELAY);

**Root cause**: When a browser tab is created, the PTY's shell pro...[truncated]

🤖 CLAUDE:
Now I see the full picture. Two root causes:

1. **Webview WebContents steals system-level focus** — DOM `blur()` in useEffect runs too late (after paint). The webview's Chromium-level input routing still intercepts keyboard before xterm gets it.

2. **Shell prompt data lost** — PTY `terminal:data` IPC event can arrive before Terminal's `handleData` listener is registered (race between IPC delivery and React useEffect). `pendingBuffer` is empty, lazy init shows blank terminal.

```
     1→import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback, memo } from 'react';
     2→import { useWorkspaceStore } from '../../store/useWorkspaceStore';
     3→import { RotateCcw, ArrowLeft, ArrowRight, Globe, TerminalSquare, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
     4→import Terminal from './Terminal';
     5→
     6→interface BrowserTabProps {
     7→  tabId: string;
     8→  url: string;
     9→  active: boolean;
    10→  isActiveProject: boolean;
    11→  terminalId?: string;
    12→  terminalName?: string;
    13→  activeView?: 'browser' | 'terminal';
    14→  cwd: string;
    15→}
    16→
    17→function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
    18→  const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
    19→  const initialUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
    20→  const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(initialUrl);
    21→  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    22→  const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    23→  const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
    24→  const updateTabUrl = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.updateTabUrl);
    25→  const setBrowserActiveView = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.setBrowserActiveView);
    26→
    27→  // Sync address bar when url prop changes (ignore about:blank)
    28→  useEffect(() => {
    29→    if (url && url !== 'about:blank') {
    30→      setAddressValue(url);
    31→    }
    32→  }, [url]);
    33→
    34→  // Webview event listeners
    35→  useEffect(() => {
    36→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    37→    if (!webview) return;
    38→
    39→    const handleDomReady = () => setIsReady(true);
    40→    const handleStartLoading = () => {
    41→      setIsLoading(true);
    42→      setLoadError(null);
    43→    };
    44→    const handleStopLoading = () => setIsLoading(false);
    45→    const handleNavigate = (e: any) => {
    46→      // Skip about:blank — don't overwrite real URL in store
    47→      if (e.url === 'about:blank') return;
    48→      setAddressValue(e.url);
    49→      updateTabUrl(tabId, e.url);
    50→    };
    51→    const handleFailLoad = (e: any) => {
    52→      // -3 = ERR_ABORTED (user navigated away / view switched) — benign
    53→      // 0 = no error
    54→      if (e.errorCode === -3 || e.errorCode === 0) return;
    55→      setLoadError(`${e.errorDescription || 'Connection failed'} (${e.validatedURL})`);
    56→      setIsLoading(false);
    57→    };
    58→
    59→    webview.addEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    60→    webview.addEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    61→    webview.addEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    62→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    63→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    64→    webview.addEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    65→
    66→    return () => {
    67→      webview.removeEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    68→      webview.removeEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    69→      webview.removeEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    70→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    71→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    72→      webview.removeEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    73→    };
    74→  }, [tabId, updateTabUrl]);
    75→
    76→  const handleAddressSubmit = useCallback((e: React.FormEvent) => {
    77→    e.preventDefault();
    78→    let navigateUrl = addressValue.trim();
    79→    if (!navigateUrl) return;
    80→
    81→    if (!navigateUrl.match(/^https?:\/\//)) {
    82→      navigateUrl = 'http://' + navigateUrl;
    83→    }
    84→
    85→    setAddressValue(navigateUrl);
    86→    updateTabUrl(tabId, navigateUrl);
    87→    setLoadError(null);
    88→
    89→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    90→    if (webview && isReady) {
    91→      webview.src = navigateUrl;
    92→    }
    93→  }, [addressValue, tabId, updateTabUrl, isReady]);
    94→
    95→  const handleRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    96→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    97→    if (webview && isReady) {
    98→      setLoadError(null);
    99→      webview.reload();
   100→    }
   101→  }, [isReady]);
   102→
   103→  const handleGoBack = useCallback(() => {
   104→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   105→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoBack()) {
   106→      webview.goBack();
   107→    }
   108→  }, [isReady]);
   109→
   110→  const handleGoForward = useCallback(() => {
   111→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   112→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoForward()) {
   113→      webview.goForward();
   114→    }
   115→  }, [isReady]);
   116→
   117→  const isVisible = active && isActiveProject;
   118→  const isBrowserView = activeView === 'browser';
   119→  const isTerminalView = activeView === 'terminal';
   120→
   121→  // Blur webview when switching to terminal view — webview is a separate WebContents
   122→  // that holds keyboard focus even with visibility:hidden, stealing input from xterm.js
   123→  useEffect(() => {
   124→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   125→    if (!webview) return;
   126→
   127→    if (isTerminalView && isVisible) {
   128→      webview.blur();
   129→    }
   130→  }, [isTerminalView, isVisible]);
   131→
   132→  return (
   133→    <div
   134→      style={{
   135→        position: 'absolute',
   136→        inset: 0,
   137→        display: 'flex',
   138→        flexDirection: 'column',
   139→        visibility: isVisible ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
   140→        pointerEvents: isVisible ? 'auto' : 'none',
   141→        zIndex: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
   142→      }}
   143→    >
   144→      {/* Toolbar - 30px */}
   145→      <div
   146→        style={{
   147→          height: '30px',
   148→          minHeight: '30px',
   149→          display: 'flex',
   150→          alignItems: 'center',
   151→          gap: '4px',
   152→          padding: '0 8px',
   153→          backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
   154→          borderBottom: '1px solid #333',
   155→        }}
   156→      >
   157→        <button
   158→          onClick={handleGoBack}
   159→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   160→          title="Back"
   161→        >
   162→          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
   163→        </button>
   164→        <button
   165→          onClick={handleGoForward}
   166→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   167→          title="Forward"
   168→        >
   169→          <ArrowRight size={14} />
   170→        </button>
   171→        <button
   172→          onClick={handleRefresh}
   173→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   174→          title="Refresh"
   175→        >
   176→          <RotateCcw size={14} className={isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />
   177→        </button>
   178→
   179→        <form onSubmit={handleAddressSubmit} style={{ flex: 1 }}>
   180→          <input
   181→            type="text"
   182→            value={addressValue}
   183→            onChange={(e) => setAddressValue(e.target.value)}
   184→            onFocus={(e) => e.target.select()}
   185→            style={{
   186→              width: '100%',
   187→              height: '22px',
   188→              backgroundColor: '#252525',
   189→              border: `1px solid ${loadError ? '#ef4444' : '#444'}`,
   190→              borderRadius: '4px',
   191→              color: '#ccc',
   192→              fontSize: '12px',
   193→              padding: '0 8px',
   194→              outline: 'none',
   195→            }}
   196→            placeholder="http://localhost:3000"
   197→          />
   198→        </form>
   199→
   200→        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '2px', marginLeft: '4px' }}>
   201→          <button
   202→            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'browser')}
   203→            style={{
   204→              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
   205→              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
   206→              backgroundColor: isBrowserView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
   207→              color: isBrowserView ? '#fff' : '#888', transition: 'all 0.15s',
   208→            }}
   209→            title="Browser view"
   210→          >
   211→            <Globe size={12} />
   212→            <span>Browser</span>
   213→          </button>
   214→          <button
   215→            onClick={() => setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'terminal')}
   216→            style={{
   217→              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
   218→              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
   219→              backgroundColor: isTerminalView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
   220→              color: isTerminalView ? '#fff' : '#888', transition: 'all 0.15s',
   221→            }}
   222→            title="Terminal view"
   223→          >
   224→            <TerminalSquare size={12} />
   225→            <span>Term</span>
   226→          </button>
   227→        </div>
   228→      </div>
   229→
   230→      {/* Content area */}
   231→      <div style={{ flex: 1, position: 'relative' }}>
   232→        {/* Webview — src set directly, errors handled via did-fail-load */}
   233→        <div
   234→          style={{
   235→            position: 'absolute',
   236→            inset: 0,
   237→            visibility: isBrowserView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
   238→            pointerEvents: isBrowserView ? 'auto' : 'none',
   239→            zIndex: isBrowserView ? 1 : 0,
   240→          }}
   241→        >
   242→          <webview
   243→            ref={webviewRef}
   244→            src={initialUrl}
   245→            style={{ width: '100%', height: '100%', border: 'none' }}
   246→            {...{ allowpopups: '' } as any}
   247→          />
   248→
   249→          {/* Error overlay */}
   250→          {loadError && isBrowserView && (
   251→            <div
   252→              style={{
   253→                position: 'absolute', inset: 0, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column',
   254→                alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a', gap: '12px',
   255→              }}
   256→            >
   257→              <AlertTriangle size={32} color="#ef4444" />
   258→              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '13px', textAlign: 'center', maxWidth: '400px', padding: '0 20px' }}>
   259→                {loadError}
   260→              </div>
   261→              <button
   262→                onClick={handleRefresh}
   263→                style={{
   264→                  padding: '6px 16px', backgroundColor: '#333', border: '1px solid #555',
   265→                  borderRadius: '6px', color: '#ccc', fontSize: '12px', cursor: 'pointer',
   266→                }}
   267→              >
   268→                Retry
   269→              </button>
   270→            </div>
   271→          )}
   272→        </div>
   273→
   274→        {/* Embedded Terminal */}
   275→        {terminalId && (
   276→          <div
   277→            style={{
   278→              position: 'absolute',
   279→              inset: 0,
   280→              visibility: isTerminalView ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
   281→              pointerEvents: isTerminalView ? 'auto' : 'none',
   282→              zIndex: isTerminalView ? 1 : 0,
   283→            }}
   284→          >
   285→            <Terminal
   286→              tabId={terminalId}
   287→              cwd={cwd}
   288→              active={active && isTerminalView}
   289→              isActiveProject={isActiveProject}
   290→            />
   291→          </div>
   292→        )}
   293→      </div>
   294→    </div>
   295→  );
   296→}
   297→
   298→export default memo(BrowserTab);
   299→
```

🤖 CLAUDE:
The test found the real issue: the output shows `[Process completed]` (exactly 19 chars) — the **PTY exits immediately** for browser tabs. The shell starts and dies before the terminal even activates. The whole approach of creating a PTY eagerly for browser tabs is wrong.

The fix: **don't create PTY for browser tabs until the user switches to terminal view**.

📝 Создание (/Users/fedor/Desktop/custom-terminal/auto/sandbox/diag-pty.js)
```
/**
 * Diagnostic: Why does browser tab PTY exit?
 * Checks PTY creation and exit logs from main process.
 */
const { launch } = require('../core/launcher')
const electron = require('../core/electron')

async function main() {
  console.log('[DIAG] Starting app...')
  const { app, page, mainProcessLogs } = await launch({
    logConsole: false,
    logMainProcess: false,
    waitForReady: 4000
  })

  try {
    await electron.focusWindow(app)
    await page.waitForTimeout(3000)

    // Create a browser tab
    console.log('[DIAG] Creating browser tab...')
    await page.evaluate(() => {
      const store = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      store?.createBrowserTab?.(store?.activeProjectId)
    })
    await page.waitForTimeout(5000) // Wait longer to catch PTY exit

    // Check tab state
    const tabState = await page.evaluate(() => {
      const store = window.useWorkspaceStore?.getState?.()
      const proj = store?.openProjects?.get?.(store?.activeProjectId)
      const tab = proj?.tabs?.get?.(proj?.activeTabId)
      return tab ? { id: tab.id, tabType: tab.tabType, pid: tab.pid } : null
    })
    console.log('[DIAG] Tab state:', JSON.stringify(tabState))

    // Dump PTY-related main process logs
    console.log('\n=== MAIN PROCESS PTY LOGS ===')
    for (const log of mainProcessLogs) {
      if (log.includes('PTY:') || log.includes('[terminal:create]') || log.includes('pty.spawn') || log.includes('PERF:main')) {
        console.log(log)
      }
    }
    console.log('=== END ===\n')

  } finally {
    await app.close()
  }
}

main().catch(err => { console.error(err.message); process.exit(1) })

```

🤖 CLAUDE:
Нашёл. Причина очевидна:

```
cwd=__unset__new_project_1770875324588_cvfvsg
exitCode={"exitCode":1,"signal":0}
```

**PTY получает `cwd=__unset__new_project_1770875324588_cvfvsg`** — это не путь, это значение-маркер `__unset__` + projectId. Шелл пытается `cd` в несуществующую директорию и умирает с exitCode 1.

Проблема в `createBrowserTab`:

🤖 CLAUDE:

```

     1→import React, { useRef, useState, useEffect, useCallback, memo } from 'react';
     2→import { useWorkspaceStore } from '../../store/useWorkspaceStore';
     3→import { RotateCcw, ArrowLeft, ArrowRight, Globe, TerminalSquare, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
     4→import Terminal from './Terminal';
     5→
     6→interface BrowserTabProps {
     7→  tabId: string;
     8→  url: string;
     9→  active: boolean;
    10→  isActiveProject: boolean;
    11→  terminalId?: string;
    12→  terminalName?: string;
    13→  activeView?: 'browser' | 'terminal';
    14→  cwd: string;
    15→}
    16→
    17→function BrowserTab({ tabId, url, active, isActiveProject, terminalId, terminalName, activeView = 'browser', cwd }: BrowserTabProps) {
    18→  const webviewRef = useRef<any>(null);
    19→  const initialUrl = url || 'http://localhost:3000';
    20→  const [addressValue, setAddressValue] = useState(initialUrl);
    21→  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    22→  const [loadError, setLoadError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    23→  const [isReady, setIsReady] = useState(false);
    24→  const updateTabUrl = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.updateTabUrl);
    25→  const setBrowserActiveView = useWorkspaceStore((s) => s.setBrowserActiveView);
    26→
    27→  // Sync address bar when url prop changes (ignore about:blank)
    28→  useEffect(() => {
    29→    if (url && url !== 'about:blank') {
    30→      setAddressValue(url);
    31→    }
    32→  }, [url]);
    33→
    34→  // Webview event listeners
    35→  useEffect(() => {
    36→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    37→    if (!webview) return;
    38→
    39→    const handleDomReady = () => setIsReady(true);
    40→    const handleStartLoading = () => {
    41→      setIsLoading(true);
    42→      setLoadError(null);
    43→    };
    44→    const handleStopLoading = () => setIsLoading(false);
    45→    const handleNavigate = (e: any) => {
    46→      // Skip about:blank — don't overwrite real URL in store
    47→      if (e.url === 'about:blank') return;
    48→      setAddressValue(e.url);
    49→      updateTabUrl(tabId, e.url);
    50→    };
    51→    const handleFailLoad = (e: any) => {
    52→      // -3 = ERR_ABORTED (user navigated away / view switched) — benign
    53→      // 0 = no error
    54→      if (e.errorCode === -3 || e.errorCode === 0) return;
    55→      setLoadError(`${e.errorDescription || 'Connection failed'} (${e.validatedURL})`);
    56→      setIsLoading(false);
    57→    };
    58→
    59→    webview.addEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    60→    webview.addEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    61→    webview.addEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    62→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    63→    webview.addEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    64→    webview.addEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    65→
    66→    return () => {
    67→      webview.removeEventListener('dom-ready', handleDomReady);
    68→      webview.removeEventListener('did-start-loading', handleStartLoading);
    69→      webview.removeEventListener('did-stop-loading', handleStopLoading);
    70→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate', handleNavigate);
    71→      webview.removeEventListener('did-navigate-in-page', handleNavigate);
    72→      webview.removeEventListener('did-fail-load', handleFailLoad);
    73→    };
    74→  }, [tabId, updateTabUrl]);
    75→
    76→  const handleAddressSubmit = useCallback((e: React.FormEvent) => {
    77→    e.preventDefault();
    78→    let navigateUrl = addressValue.trim();
    79→    if (!navigateUrl) return;
    80→
    81→    if (!navigateUrl.match(/^https?:\/\//)) {
    82→      navigateUrl = 'http://' + navigateUrl;
    83→    }
    84→
    85→    setAddressValue(navigateUrl);
    86→    updateTabUrl(tabId, navigateUrl);
    87→    setLoadError(null);
    88→
    89→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    90→    if (webview && isReady) {
    91→      webview.src = navigateUrl;
    92→    }
    93→  }, [addressValue, tabId, updateTabUrl, isReady]);
    94→
    95→  const handleRefresh = useCallback(() => {
    96→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
    97→    if (webview && isReady) {
    98→      setLoadError(null);
    99→      webview.reload();
   100→    }
   101→  }, [isReady]);
   102→
   103→  const handleGoBack = useCallback(() => {
   104→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   105→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoBack()) {
   106→      webview.goBack();
   107→    }
   108→  }, [isReady]);
   109→
   110→  const handleGoForward = useCallback(() => {
   111→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   112→    if (webview && isReady && webview.canGoForward()) {
   113→      webview.goForward();
   114→    }
   115→  }, [isReady]);
   116→
   117→  const isVisible = active && isActiveProject;
   118→  const isBrowserView = activeView === 'browser';
   119→  const isTerminalView = activeView === 'terminal';
   120→
   121→  // Blur webview when switching to terminal view — webview is a separate WebContents
   122→  // that holds Chromium-level keyboard focus even with visibility:hidden.
   123→  // useEffect runs after paint — serves as fallback for persisted state restoration.
   124→  useEffect(() => {
   125→    const webview = webviewRef.current;
   126→    if (!webview) return;
   127→
   128→    if (isTerminalView && isVisible) {
   129→      webview.blur();
   130→    }
   131→  }, [isTerminalView, isVisible]);
   132→
   133→  // Synchronous view switch handlers — blur/focus webview BEFORE React re-render
   134→  // to prevent Chromium input routing race (useEffect alone is too late)
   135→  const handleSwitchToTerminal = useCallback(() => {
   136→    webviewRef.current?.blur();
   137→    setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'terminal');
   138→  }, [tabId, setBrowserActiveView]);
   139→
   140→  const handleSwitchToBrowser = useCallback(() => {
   141→    setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'browser');
   142→  }, [tabId, setBrowserActiveView]);
   143→
   144→  return (
   145→    <div
   146→      style={{
   147→        position: 'absolute',
   148→        inset: 0,
   149→        display: 'flex',
   150→        flexDirection: 'column',
   151→        visibility: isVisible ? 'inherit' : 'hidden',
   152→        pointerEvents: isVisible ? 'auto' : 'none',
   153→        zIndex: isVisible ? 1 : 0,
   154→      }}
   155→    >
   156→      {/* Toolbar - 30px */}
   157→      <div
   158→        style={{
   159→          height: '30px',
   160→          minHeight: '30px',
   161→          display: 'flex',
   162→          alignItems: 'center',
   163→          gap: '4px',
   164→          padding: '0 8px',
   165→          backgroundColor: '#1a1a1a',
   166→          borderBottom: '1px solid #333',
   167→        }}
   168→      >
   169→        <button
   170→          onClick={handleGoBack}
   171→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   172→          title="Back"
   173→        >
   174→          <ArrowLeft size={14} />
   175→        </button>
   176→        <button
   177→          onClick={handleGoForward}
   178→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   179→          title="Forward"
   180→        >
   181→          <ArrowRight size={14} />
   182→        </button>
   183→        <button
   184→          onClick={handleRefresh}
   185→          style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#888', cursor: 'pointer', padding: '2px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }}
   186→          title="Refresh"
   187→        >
   188→          <RotateCcw size={14} className={isLoading ? 'animate-spin' : ''} />
   189→        </button>
   190→
   191→        <form onSubmit={handleAddressSubmit} style={{ flex: 1 }}>
   192→          <input
   193→            type="text"
   194→            value={addressValue}
   195→            onChange={(e) => setAddressValue(e.target.value)}
   196→            onFocus={(e) => e.target.select()}
   197→            style={{
   198→              width: '100%',
   199→              height: '22px',
   200→              backgroundColor: '#252525',
   201→              border: `1px solid ${loadError ? '#ef4444' : '#444'}`,
   202→              borderRadius: '4px',
   203→              color: '#ccc',
   204→              fontSize: '12px',
   205→              padding: '0 8px',
   206→              outline: 'none',
   207→            }}
   208→            placeholder="http://localhost:3000"
   209→          />
   210→        </form>
   211→
   212→        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '2px', marginLeft: '4px' }}>
   213→          <button
   214→            onClick={handleSwitchToBrowser}
   215→            style={{
   216→              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
   217→              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
   218→              backgroundColor: isBrowserView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',
   219→              color: isBrowserView ? '#fff' : '#888', transition: 'all 0.15s',
   220→            }}
   221→            title="Browser view"
   222→          >
   223→            <Globe size={12} />
   224→            <span>Browser</span>
   225→          </button>
   226→          <button
   227→            onClick={handleSwitchToTerminal}
   228→            style={{
   229→              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '4px', padding: '2px 8px', height: '22px',
   230→              borderRadius: '4px', border: 'none', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer',
   231→              backgroundColor: isTerminalView ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.15)' : 'transparent',

   233→            }}
   234→            title="Terminal view"

   237→            <span>Term</span>

   241→
   242→      {/* Content area */}
   243→      <div style={{ flex: 1, position: 'relative' }}>
   244→        {/* Webview — src set directly, errors handled via did-fail-load */}

   246→          style={{

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   - User reported `ERR_ABORTED (-3)` error when switching to Terminal view in browser tab, and inability to type in the embedded terminal
   - User wanted the root cause found and fixed properly (no hacks/костыли)
   - User requested that the "Term" button in BrowserTab toolbar should show a green dot indicator when there's an active running process in the embedded terminal, matching the behavior of regular terminal tabs

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - Electron `<webview>` is a separate WebContents that holds Chromium-level keyboard focus even with `visibility:hidden` and `pointerEvents:none` — requires explicit `.blur()` to release
   - `webview.blur()` in React `useEffect` runs after paint (too late for focus race) — synchronous blur in click handler is needed
   - PTY process dies with exitCode 1 when spawned with invalid CWD like `__unset__<projectId>` — the `__unset__` prefix is a sentinel value that's truthy but not a real filesystem path
   - Process indicator in TabBar uses IPC events: `terminal:command-started`, `terminal:command-finished`, and initial sync via `terminal:getCommandState`
   - The dot indicator is 6x6px circular, green (#4ade80) with glow shadow `0 0 4px rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.5)`

3. Files and Code Sections:

   - **`src/renderer/components/Workspace/BrowserTab.tsx`** — Main browser tab component with webview + embedded terminal
     - Added `ipcRenderer` import, `hasProcess` state, IPC listener for process tracking
     - Added `webview.blur()` useEffect for terminal view switch (fallback)
     - Added synchronous `handleSwitchToTerminal` / `handleSwitchToBrowser` handlers that blur webview BEFORE React re-render
     - Added green dot indicator before TerminalSquare icon in Term button
     ```tsx
     const { ipcRenderer } = window.require('electron');
     
     // Inside component:
     const [hasProcess, setHasProcess] = useState(false);
     
     // Track running process in embedded terminal
     useEffect(() => {
       const tid = terminalId || tabId;
       const onStarted = (_: any, startedTabId: string) => {
         if (startedTabId === tid) setHasProcess(true);
       };
       const onFinished = (_: any, finishedTabId: string) => {
         if (finishedTabId === tid) setHasProcess(false);
       };
       ipcRenderer.on('terminal:command-started', onStarted);
       ipcRenderer.on('terminal:command-finished', onFinished);
       ipcRenderer.invoke('terminal:getCommandState', tid).then((state: any) => {
         if (state?.isRunning) setHasProcess(true);
       }).catch(() => {});
       return () => {
         ipcRenderer.removeListener('terminal:command-started', onStarted);
         ipcRenderer.removeListener('terminal:command-finished', onFinished);
       };
     }, [terminalId, tabId]);
     
     // Synchronous view switch handlers
     const handleSwitchToTerminal = useCallback(() => {
       webviewRef.current?.blur();
       setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'terminal');
     }, [tabId, setBrowserActiveView]);
     
     const handleSwitchToBrowser = useCallback(() => {
       setBrowserActiveView(tabId, 'browser');
     }, [tabId, setBrowserActiveView]);
     
     // In Term button JSX:
     {hasProcess && (
       <span style={{
         display: 'block', width: '6px', height: '6px', borderRadius: '50%',
         backgroundColor: '#4ade80',
         boxShadow: '0 0 4px rgba(74, 222, 128, 0.5)',
         flexShrink: 0,
       }} />
     )}
     <TerminalSquare size={12} />
     <span>Term</span>
     ```

   - **`src/renderer/store/useWorkspaceStore.ts`** — Zustand store
     - Fixed `createBrowserTab` CWD handling to filter out `__unset__` prefix
     ```typescript
     createBrowserTab: async (projectId) => {
       const { openProjects, createTab } = get();
       const workspace = openProjects.get(projectId);
       const projectPath = workspace?.projectPath;
       const cwd = (projectPath && !projectPath.startsWith('__unset__')) ? projectPath : (process.env.HOME || '~');
       return createTab(projectId, 'Browser', cwd, { tabType: 'browser', url: 'http://localhost:3000' });
     },
     ```

   - **`src/main/main.js`** — Electron main process

     // Line 771

     // Line 923

     ```

4. Errors and fixes:
   - **ERR_ABORTED (-3) on view switch**: Electron internal GUEST_VIEW_MANAGER_CALL error — benign console noise, already handled by `did-fail-load` handler ignoring errorCode -3
   - **Terminal can't receive input (webview focus stealing)**: Fixed by adding `webview.blur()` both in useEffect (fallback) and synchronously in `handleSwitchToTerminal` click handler
   - **SIGWINCH hack (WRONG approach)**: Added resize trick to force shell prompt redraw — user told me this was a hack/костыль. Removed.
   - **Lazy PTY creation (CATASTROPHIC)**: Skipped PTY creation for browser tabs in createTab, tried to create lazily in Terminal.tsx — BROKE ALL TERMINALS showing [Process completed]. User was very angry: "блять теперь у всех вообще всех терминало [Process completed]". User reverted all changes themselves.
     - Root cause: my lazy PTY code in Terminal.tsx was interfering with ALL terminals, not just browser tabs
   - **Real root cause found**: PTY dying because `workspace.projectPath` = `__unset__new_project_...` which is truthy but not a valid filesystem path. Shell spawned with this as CWD exits with code 1.
     - Fix: Check for `__unset__` prefix in `createBrowserTab` before using projectPath as CWD
   - **Test `testMarker` not in scope**: `page.evaluate` runs in browser context, template literal with `testMarker` variable was not accessible. Fixed by passing as argument object.

5. Problem Solving:
   - Diagnosed webview focus stealing via Electron WebContents architecture knowledge
   - Used diagnostic script (`diag-pty.js`) to capture main process PTY logs, which revealed the `__unset__` CWD as the true root cause of PTY death
   - All PTY exits had `cwd=__unset__new_project_1770875324588_cvfvsg` and `exitCode={"exitCode":1,"signal":0}`
   - After CWD fix, new browser tabs spawn PTY with `cwd=/Users/fedor` and PTY stays alive (no PTY:EXIT)
   - Terminal prompt now displays correctly (27 chars: `fedor@MacBook-Air-Fedor ~ %`)
